\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!enableSoundPositionIndication@{enableSoundPositionIndication}}
\index{enableSoundPositionIndication@{enableSoundPositionIndication}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableSoundPositionIndication()}{enableSoundPositionIndication()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::enable\+Sound\+Position\+Indication (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Enables/\+Disables stereo panning for remote users.

Ensure that you call this method before join\+Channel to enable stereo panning for remote users so that the local user can track the position of a remote user by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac5c3755a1cca201b2a8066af07a653f6}{set\+Remote\+Voice\+Position}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & Sets whether or not to enable stereo panning for remote users\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: enables stereo panning.
\item false\+: disables stereo panning.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac5c3755a1cca201b2a8066af07a653f6}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac5c3755a1cca201b2a8066af07a653f6}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setRemoteVoicePosition@{setRemoteVoicePosition}}
\index{setRemoteVoicePosition@{setRemoteVoicePosition}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setRemoteVoicePosition()}{setRemoteVoicePosition()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Remote\+Voice\+Position (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uid\+\_\+t}]{uid,  }\item[{double}]{pan,  }\item[{double}]{gain }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets the sound position and gain of a remote user.

When the local user calls this method to set the sound position of a remote user, the sound difference between the left and right channels allows the local user to track the real-\/time position of the remote user, creating a real sense of space. This method applies to massively multiplayer online games, such as Battle Royale games.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item For this method to work, enable stereo panning for remote users by calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac3f53f474760a834fef050937c4cf7fa}{enable\+Sound\+Position\+Indication}} method before joining a channel.
\item This method requires hardware support. For the best sound positioning, we recommend using a wired headset.
\item Ensure that you call this method after joining a channel.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em uid} & The ID of the remote user. \\
\hline
{\em pan} & The sound position of the remote user. The value ranges from -\/1.\+0 to 1.\+0\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0.\+0\+: the remote sound comes from the front.
\item -\/1.\+0\+: the remote sound comes from the left.
\item 1.\+0\+: the remote sound comes from the right. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em gain} & Gain of the remote user. The value ranges from 0.\+0 to 100.\+0. The default value is 100.\+0 (the original gain of the remote user). The smaller the value, the less the gain.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac710640d68fa42f3130d1aaf3b8d3c4c}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac710640d68fa42f3130d1aaf3b8d3c4c}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a577b68f53ed63771da80ec8901ed93e5}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a577b68f53ed63771da80ec8901ed93e5}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setVoiceBeautifierPreset@{setVoiceBeautifierPreset}}
\index{setVoiceBeautifierPreset@{setVoiceBeautifierPreset}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setVoiceBeautifierPreset()}{setVoiceBeautifierPreset()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Preset (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{V\+O\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+B\+E\+A\+U\+T\+I\+F\+I\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+S\+ET}]{preset }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets an S\+DK preset voice beautifier effect.

Call this method to set an S\+DK preset voice beautifier effect for the local user who sends an audio stream. After setting a voice beautifier effect, all users in the channel can hear the effect.

You can set different voice beautifier effects for different scenarios. See {\itshape Set the Voice Beautifier and Audio Effects}.

To achieve better audio effect quality, Agora recommends calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7c9aef3f4c8f9cb62e5ae3c4aa7ed81a}{set\+Audio\+Profile}} and setting the {\ttfamily scenario} parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+S\+C\+E\+N\+A\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+I\+N\+G(3)} and the {\ttfamily profile} parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y(4)} or {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+E\+R\+E\+O(5)} before calling this method.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item You can call this method either before or after joining a channel.
\item Do not set the {\ttfamily profile} parameter of \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7c9aef3f4c8f9cb62e5ae3c4aa7ed81a}{set\+Audio\+Profile}} to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+P\+E\+E\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+N\+D\+A\+R\+D(1)} or {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+O\+T(6)}; otherwise, this method call fails.
\item This method works best with the human voice. Agora does not recommend using this method for audio containing music.
\item After calling this method, Agora recommends not calling the following methods, because they can override \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a9e5a3c34818abd26b0d0a9434f7ce4ca}{set\+Audio\+Effect\+Parameters}}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a6111d2648909601c976b0190fe6de798}{set\+Audio\+Effect\+Preset}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a577b68f53ed63771da80ec8901ed93e5}{set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Preset}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a43616f919e0906279dff5648830ce31a}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Pitch}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a8c75994eb06ab26a1704715ec76e0189}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Equalization}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a4d1d1309f97f3c430a1aa2d060bb7316}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Reverb}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_afe1e3302f3d1f670bc5cdaa870fe95e8}{set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Parameters}}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em preset} & The options for S\+DK preset voice beautifier effects\+: \#\+V\+O\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+B\+E\+A\+U\+T\+I\+F\+I\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+S\+ET.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a6111d2648909601c976b0190fe6de798}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a6111d2648909601c976b0190fe6de798}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setAudioEffectPreset@{setAudioEffectPreset}}
\index{setAudioEffectPreset@{setAudioEffectPreset}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setAudioEffectPreset()}{setAudioEffectPreset()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Audio\+Effect\+Preset (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+E\+F\+F\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+S\+ET}]{preset }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets an S\+DK preset audio effect.

Call this method to set an S\+DK preset audio effect for the local user who sends an audio stream. This audio effect does not change the gender characteristics of the original voice. After setting an audio effect, all users in the channel can hear the effect.

You can set different audio effects for different scenarios. See {\itshape Set the Voice Beautifier and Audio Effects}.

To achieve better audio effect quality, Agora recommends calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7c9aef3f4c8f9cb62e5ae3c4aa7ed81a}{set\+Audio\+Profile}} and setting the {\ttfamily scenario} parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+S\+C\+E\+N\+A\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+I\+N\+G(3)} before calling this method.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item You can call this method either before or after joining a channel.
\item Do not set the profile {\ttfamily parameter} of {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Profile} to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+P\+E\+E\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+N\+D\+A\+R\+D(1)} or {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+O\+T(6)}; otherwise, this method call fails.
\item This method works best with the human voice. Agora does not recommend using this method for audio containing music.
\item If you call this method and set the {\ttfamily preset} parameter to enumerators except {\ttfamily R\+O\+O\+M\+\_\+\+A\+C\+O\+U\+S\+T\+I\+C\+S\+\_\+3\+D\+\_\+\+V\+O\+I\+CE} or {\ttfamily P\+I\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+C\+O\+R\+R\+E\+C\+T\+I\+ON}, do not call \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a9e5a3c34818abd26b0d0a9434f7ce4ca}{set\+Audio\+Effect\+Parameters}}; otherwise, {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Effect\+Parameters} overrides this method.
\item After calling this method, Agora recommends not calling the following methods, because they can override {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Effect\+Preset}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a577b68f53ed63771da80ec8901ed93e5}{set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Preset}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a43616f919e0906279dff5648830ce31a}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Pitch}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a8c75994eb06ab26a1704715ec76e0189}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Equalization}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a4d1d1309f97f3c430a1aa2d060bb7316}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Reverb}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_afe1e3302f3d1f670bc5cdaa870fe95e8}{set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Parameters}}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Voice\+Conversion\+Preset (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{V\+O\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+S\+ET}]{preset }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets an S\+DK preset voice conversion.

Call this method to set an S\+DK preset voice conversion for the local user who sends an audio stream. After setting an voice conversion, all users in the channel can hear the effect.

You can set different voice conversion for different scenarios. See {\itshape Set the Voice Beautifier and Audio Effects}.

To achieve better voice conversion quality, Agora recommends calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7c9aef3f4c8f9cb62e5ae3c4aa7ed81a}{set\+Audio\+Profile}} and setting the {\ttfamily scenario} parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+S\+C\+E\+N\+A\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+I\+N\+G(3)} before calling this method.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item You can call this method either before or after joining a channel.
\item Do not set the profile {\ttfamily parameter} of {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Profile} to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+P\+E\+E\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+N\+D\+A\+R\+D(1)} or {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+O\+T(6)}; otherwise, this method call fails.
\item This method works best with the human voice. Agora does not recommend using this method for audio containing music.
\item If you call this method and set the {\ttfamily preset} parameter to enumerators,
\item After calling this method, Agora recommends not calling the following methods, because they can override {\ttfamily set\+Voice\+Conversion\+Preset}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a577b68f53ed63771da80ec8901ed93e5}{set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Preset}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a6111d2648909601c976b0190fe6de798}{set\+Audio\+Effect\+Preset}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a43616f919e0906279dff5648830ce31a}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Pitch}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a539a3345c38cc5d1d26edda69cf0661c}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Formant}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a8c75994eb06ab26a1704715ec76e0189}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Equalization}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a4d1d1309f97f3c430a1aa2d060bb7316}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Reverb}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_afe1e3302f3d1f670bc5cdaa870fe95e8}{set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Parameters}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a9e5a3c34818abd26b0d0a9434f7ce4ca}{set\+Audio\+Effect\+Parameters}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setAudioEffectParameters()}{setAudioEffectParameters()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Audio\+Effect\+Parameters (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+E\+F\+F\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+S\+ET}]{preset,  }\item[{int}]{param1,  }\item[{int}]{param2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets parameters for S\+DK preset audio effects.

Call this method to set the following parameters for the local user who send an audio stream\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 3D voice effect\+: Sets the cycle period of the 3D voice effect.
\item Pitch correction effect\+: Sets the basic mode and tonic pitch of the pitch correction effect. Different songs have different modes and tonic pitches. Agora recommends bounding this method with interface elements to enable users to adjust the pitch correction interactively.
\end{DoxyItemize}

After setting parameters, all users in the channel can hear the relevant effect.

You can call this method directly or after \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a6111d2648909601c976b0190fe6de798}{set\+Audio\+Effect\+Preset}}. If you call this method after \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a6111d2648909601c976b0190fe6de798}{set\+Audio\+Effect\+Preset}}, ensure that you set the preset parameter of {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Effect\+Preset} to {\ttfamily R\+O\+O\+M\+\_\+\+A\+C\+O\+U\+S\+T\+I\+C\+S\+\_\+3\+D\+\_\+\+V\+O\+I\+CE} or {\ttfamily P\+I\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+C\+O\+R\+R\+E\+C\+T\+I\+ON} and then call this method to set the same enumerator; otherwise, this method overrides {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Effect\+Preset}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item You can call this method either before or after joining a channel.
\item To achieve better audio effect quality, Agora recommends calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7c9aef3f4c8f9cb62e5ae3c4aa7ed81a}{set\+Audio\+Profile}} and setting the {\ttfamily scenario} parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+S\+C\+E\+N\+A\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+I\+N\+G(3)} before calling this method.
\item Do not set the {\ttfamily profile} parameter of \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7c9aef3f4c8f9cb62e5ae3c4aa7ed81a}{set\+Audio\+Profile}} to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+P\+E\+E\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+N\+D\+A\+R\+D(1)} or {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+O\+T(6)}; otherwise, this method call fails.
\item This method works best with the human voice. Agora does not recommend using this method for audio containing music.
\item After calling this method, Agora recommends not calling the following methods, because they can override {\ttfamily set\+Audio\+Effect\+Parameters}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a6111d2648909601c976b0190fe6de798}{set\+Audio\+Effect\+Preset}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a577b68f53ed63771da80ec8901ed93e5}{set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Preset}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a43616f919e0906279dff5648830ce31a}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Pitch}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a8c75994eb06ab26a1704715ec76e0189}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Equalization}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a4d1d1309f97f3c430a1aa2d060bb7316}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Reverb}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_afe1e3302f3d1f670bc5cdaa870fe95e8}{set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Parameters}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em preset} & The options for S\+DK preset audio effects\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 3D voice effect\+: {\ttfamily R\+O\+O\+M\+\_\+\+A\+C\+O\+U\+S\+T\+I\+C\+S\+\_\+3\+D\+\_\+\+V\+O\+I\+CE}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Call \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7c9aef3f4c8f9cb62e5ae3c4aa7ed81a}{set\+Audio\+Profile}} and set the {\ttfamily profile} parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+N\+D\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+S\+T\+E\+R\+E\+O(3)} or {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+E\+R\+E\+O(5)} before setting this enumerator; otherwise, the enumerator setting does not take effect.
\item If the 3D voice effect is enabled, users need to use stereo audio playback devices to hear the anticipated voice effect.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Pitch correction effect\+: {\ttfamily P\+I\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+C\+O\+R\+R\+E\+C\+T\+I\+ON}. To achieve better audio effect quality, Agora recommends calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7c9aef3f4c8f9cb62e5ae3c4aa7ed81a}{set\+Audio\+Profile}} and setting the {\ttfamily profile} parameter to {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y(4)} or {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+E\+R\+E\+O(5)} before setting this enumerator. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em param1} & 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If you set {\ttfamily preset} to {\ttfamily R\+O\+O\+M\+\_\+\+A\+C\+O\+U\+S\+T\+I\+C\+S\+\_\+3\+D\+\_\+\+V\+O\+I\+CE}, the {\ttfamily param1} sets the cycle period of the 3D voice effect. The value range is \mbox{[}1,60\mbox{]} and the unit is a second. The default value is 10 seconds, indicating that the voice moves around you every 10 seconds.
\item If you set {\ttfamily preset} to {\ttfamily P\+I\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+C\+O\+R\+R\+E\+C\+T\+I\+ON}, {\ttfamily param1} sets the basic mode of the pitch correction effect\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily 1}\+: (Default) Natural major scale.
\item {\ttfamily 2}\+: Natural minor scale.
\item {\ttfamily 3}\+: Japanese pentatonic scale. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em param2} & 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If you set {\ttfamily preset} to {\ttfamily R\+O\+O\+M\+\_\+\+A\+C\+O\+U\+S\+T\+I\+C\+S\+\_\+3\+D\+\_\+\+V\+O\+I\+CE}, you need to set {\ttfamily param2} to {\ttfamily 0}.
\item If you set {\ttfamily preset} to {\ttfamily P\+I\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+C\+O\+R\+R\+E\+C\+T\+I\+ON}, {\ttfamily param2} sets the tonic pitch of the pitch correction effect\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily 1}\+: A
\item {\ttfamily 2}\+: A\#
\item {\ttfamily 3}\+: B
\item {\ttfamily 4}\+: (Default) C
\item {\ttfamily 5}\+: C\#
\item {\ttfamily 6}\+: D
\item {\ttfamily 7}\+: D\#
\item {\ttfamily 8}\+: E
\item {\ttfamily 9}\+: F
\item {\ttfamily 10}\+: F\#
\item {\ttfamily 11}\+: G
\item {\ttfamily 12}\+: G\#
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\\

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setVoiceBeautifierParameters()}{setVoiceBeautifierParameters()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Parameters (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{V\+O\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+B\+E\+A\+U\+T\+I\+F\+I\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+S\+ET}]{preset,  }\item[{int}]{param1,  }\item[{int}]{param2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets parameters for S\+DK preset voice beautifier effects.

Call this method to set a gender characteristic and a reverberation effect for the singing beautifier effect. This method sets parameters for the local user who sends an audio stream.

After you call this method successfully, all users in the channel can hear the relevant effect.

To achieve better audio effect quality, before you call this method, Agora recommends calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7c9aef3f4c8f9cb62e5ae3c4aa7ed81a}{set\+Audio\+Profile}}, and setting the {\ttfamily scenario} parameter as {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+S\+C\+E\+N\+A\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+I\+N\+G(3)} and the {\ttfamily profile} parameter as {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y(4)} or {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+S\+I\+C\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+E\+R\+E\+O(5)}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item You can call this method either before or after joining a channel.
\item Do not set the {\ttfamily profile} parameter of \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7c9aef3f4c8f9cb62e5ae3c4aa7ed81a}{set\+Audio\+Profile}} as {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+P\+E\+E\+C\+H\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+N\+D\+A\+R\+D(1)} or {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+O\+T(6)}; otherwise, this method call does not take effect.
\item This method works best with the human voice. Agora does not recommend using this method for audio containing music.
\item After you call this method, Agora recommends not calling the following methods, because they can override {\ttfamily set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Parameters}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a6111d2648909601c976b0190fe6de798}{set\+Audio\+Effect\+Preset}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a9e5a3c34818abd26b0d0a9434f7ce4ca}{set\+Audio\+Effect\+Parameters}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a577b68f53ed63771da80ec8901ed93e5}{set\+Voice\+Beautifier\+Preset}}

\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a8c75994eb06ab26a1704715ec76e0189}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Equalization}}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a4d1d1309f97f3c430a1aa2d060bb7316}{set\+Local\+Voice\+Reverb}}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setLogFile@{setLogFile}}
\index{setLogFile@{setLogFile}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLogFile()}{setLogFile()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Log\+File (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{file\+Path }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

{\bfseries{D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED}} Specifies an S\+DK output log file.

The log file records all log data for the S\+D\+K’s operation. Ensure that the directory for the log file exists and is writable.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Ensure that you call this method immediately after \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac71db65e66942e4e0a0550e95c16890f}{initialize}}, or the output log may not be complete.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em file\+Path} & File path of the log file. The string of the log file is in U\+T\+F-\/8.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_acfc056b4c693d134bece8e7c0f05e69f}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_acfc056b4c693d134bece8e7c0f05e69f}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setLogFilter@{setLogFilter}}
\index{setLogFilter@{setLogFilter}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLogFilter()}{setLogFilter()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Log\+Filter (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned int}]{filter }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets the output log filter level of the S\+DK.

You can use one or a combination of the filters. The log filter level follows the sequence of {\ttfamily O\+FF}, {\ttfamily C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+AL}, {\ttfamily E\+R\+R\+OR}, {\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG}, {\ttfamily I\+N\+FO}, and {\ttfamily D\+E\+B\+UG}. Choose a filter level and you will see logs preceding that filter level. For example, if you set the log filter level to {\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG}, you see the logs within levels {\ttfamily C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+AL}, {\ttfamily E\+R\+R\+OR}, and {\ttfamily W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em filter} & The log filter level\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+E\+B\+U\+G(0x80f)}\+: Output all A\+PI logs. Set your log filter as D\+E\+B\+UG if you want to get the most complete log file.
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O(0x0f)}\+: Output logs of the C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+AL, E\+R\+R\+OR, W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG, and I\+N\+FO level. We recommend setting your log filter as this level.
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+N\+G(0x0e)}\+: Output logs of the C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+AL, E\+R\+R\+OR, and W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG level.
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R(0x0c)}\+: Output logs of the C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+AL and E\+R\+R\+OR level.
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+A\+L(0x08)}\+: Output logs of the C\+R\+I\+T\+I\+C\+AL level.
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+O\+F\+F(0)}\+: Do not output any log.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_af24a402778204b60effc6b3879391c10}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_af24a402778204b60effc6b3879391c10}}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+\+N\+O\+NE (0x0000)}\+: Do not output any log file.
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+FO (0x0001)}\+: (Recommended) Output log files of the I\+N\+FO level.
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+\+W\+A\+RN (0x0002)}\+: Output log files of the W\+A\+RN level.
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR (0x0004)}\+: Output log files of the E\+R\+R\+OR level.
\item {\ttfamily L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+\+F\+A\+T\+AL (0x0008)}\+: Output log files of the F\+A\+T\+AL level.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setLogFileSize@{setLogFileSize}}
\index{setLogFileSize@{setLogFileSize}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLogFileSize()}{setLogFileSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Log\+File\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned int}]{file\+Size\+In\+K\+Bytes }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets the log file size (KB).

The S\+DK has two log files, each with a default size of 512 KB. If you set {\ttfamily file\+Size\+In\+Bytes} as 1024 KB, the S\+DK outputs log files with a total maximum size of 2 MB. If the total size of the log files exceed the set value, the new output log files overwrite the old output log files.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em file\+Size\+In\+K\+Bytes} & The S\+DK log file size (KB). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setLocalRenderMode@{setLocalRenderMode}}
\index{setLocalRenderMode@{setLocalRenderMode}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLocalRenderMode()}{setLocalRenderMode()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Local\+Render\+Mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{media\+::base\+::\+R\+E\+N\+D\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}]{render\+Mode,  }\item[{V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}]{mirror\+Mode }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Updates the display mode of the local video view.

After initializing the local video view, you can call this method to update its rendering mode. It affects only the video view that the local user sees, not the published local video stream.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Ensure that you have called \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a744003a9c0230684e985e42d14361f28}{setup\+Local\+Video}} to initialize the local video view before this method.
\item During a call, you can call this method as many times as necessary to update the local video view.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setRemoteRenderMode()}{setRemoteRenderMode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Remote\+Render\+Mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uid\+\_\+t}]{uid,  }\item[{media\+::base\+::\+R\+E\+N\+D\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}]{render\+Mode,  }\item[{V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}]{mirror\+Mode }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Updates the display mode of the video view of a remote user.

After initializing the video view of a remote user, you can call this method to update its rendering and mirror modes. This method affects only the video view that the local user sees.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Ensure that you have called \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac166814787b0a1d8da5f5c632dd7cdcf}{setup\+Remote\+Video}} to initialize the remote video view before calling this method.
\item During a call, you can call this method as many times as necessary to update the display mode of the video view of a remote user.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em uid} & ID of the remote user. \\
\hline
{\em render\+Mode} & Sets the remote display mode. See \#\+R\+E\+N\+D\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE. \\
\hline
{\em mirror\+Mode} & Sets the mirror type. See \#\+V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE.\\
\hline

If dual-\/stream mode is enabled, the subscriber can choose to receive the high-\/stream (high-\/resolution high-\/bitrate video stream) or low-\/stream (low-\/resolution low-\/bitrate video stream) video using \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7c4564b1f4a00658b4f54960ede571a9}{set\+Remote\+Video\+Stream\+Type}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\item false\+: (default) Disable the dual-\/stream mode. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a6f411291eb8b834442b44361f78fa81f}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a6f411291eb8b834442b44361f78fa81f}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setLocalPublishFallbackOption@{setLocalPublishFallbackOption}}
\index{setLocalPublishFallbackOption@{setLocalPublishFallbackOption}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLocalPublishFallbackOption()}{setLocalPublishFallbackOption()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Local\+Publish\+Fallback\+Option (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+NS}]{option }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets the fallback option for the published video stream based on the network conditions.

If {\ttfamily option} is set as \#\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+O\+N\+LY (2), the S\+DK will\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Disable the upstream video but enable audio only when the network conditions deteriorate and cannot support both video and audio.
\item Re-\/enable the video when the network conditions improve.
\end{DoxyItemize}

When the published video stream falls back to audio only or when the audio-\/only stream switches back to the video, the S\+DK triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_ace4279c4d87c23a1fecc3eb8e862a513}{on\+Local\+Publish\+Fallback\+To\+Audio\+Only}} callback.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Agora does not recommend using this method for C\+DN live streaming, because the remote C\+DN live user will have a noticeable lag when the published video stream falls back to audio only.
\item Ensure that you call this method before joining a channel.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em option} & Sets the fallback option for the published video stream\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \#\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+ED (0)\+: (Default) No fallback behavior for the published video stream when the uplink network condition is poor. The stream quality is not guaranteed.
\item \#\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+O\+N\+LY (2)\+: The published video stream falls back to audio only when the uplink network condition is poor.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_afd251e3f353a31d470ff9e60c3c3c5de}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_afd251e3f353a31d470ff9e60c3c3c5de}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setRemoteSubscribeFallbackOption@{setRemoteSubscribeFallbackOption}}
\index{setRemoteSubscribeFallbackOption@{setRemoteSubscribeFallbackOption}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setRemoteSubscribeFallbackOption()}{setRemoteSubscribeFallbackOption()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Remote\+Subscribe\+Fallback\+Option (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+NS}]{option }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets the fallback option for the remotely subscribed video stream based on the network conditions.

The default setting for {\ttfamily option} is \#\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+L\+OW (1), where the remotely subscribed video stream falls back to the low-\/stream video (low resolution and low bitrate) under poor downlink network conditions.

If {\ttfamily option} is set as \#\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+O\+N\+LY (2), the S\+DK automatically switches the video from a high-\/stream to a low-\/stream, or disables the video when the downlink network conditions cannot support both audio and video to guarantee the quality of the audio. The S\+DK monitors the network quality and restores the video stream when the network conditions improve.

When the remotely subscribed video stream falls back to audio only or when the audio-\/only stream switches back to the video stream, the S\+DK triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a7ee343146ad6e3f120bd04a7a6fdda74}{on\+Remote\+Subscribe\+Fallback\+To\+Audio\+Only}} callback.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Ensure that you call this method before joining a channel.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em option} & Sets the fallback option for the remotely subscribed video stream. See \#\+S\+T\+R\+E\+A\+M\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+L\+B\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+I\+O\+NS. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a6d91b4c3234f741d1210db9d0c6a96ba}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a6d91b4c3234f741d1210db9d0c6a96ba}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setHighPriorityUserList@{setHighPriorityUserList}}
\index{setHighPriorityUserList@{setHighPriorityUserList}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setHighPriorityUserList()}{setHighPriorityUserList()}}

\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac6fc97b54f53ebc5cc28049a04d51170}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac6fc97b54f53ebc5cc28049a04d51170}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!enableExtension@{enableExtension}}
\index{enableExtension@{enableExtension}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableExtension()}{enableExtension()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::enable\+Extension (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{provider,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{extension,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_extension_info}{Extension\+Info}} \&}]{extension\+Info,  }\item[{bool}]{enable = {\ttfamily true} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Enable/\+Disable an extension. By calling this function, you can dynamically enable/disable the extension without changing the pipeline. For example, enabling/disabling Extension\+\_\+A means the data will be adapted/bypassed by Extension\+\_\+A.

N\+O\+TE\+: For compatibility reasons, if you haven\textquotesingle{}t call register\+Extension, enable\+Extension will automatically register the specified extension. We suggest you call register\+Extension explicitly.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em provider} & The name of the extension provider, e.\+g. agora.\+io. \\
\hline
{\em extension} & The name of the extension, e.\+g. agora.\+beauty. \\
\hline
{\em extension\+Info} & The information for extension. \\
\hline
{\em enable} & Whether to enable the extension\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: (Default) Enable the extension.
\item false\+: Disable the extension.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_afd6dc645147e9d4021dfa7ff673f2b3d}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_afd6dc645147e9d4021dfa7ff673f2b3d}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setExtensionProperty@{setExtensionProperty}}
\index{setExtensionProperty@{setExtensionProperty}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setExtensionProperty()}{setExtensionProperty()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Extension\+Property (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{provider,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{extension,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_extension_info}{Extension\+Info}} \&}]{extension\+Info,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{key,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets the properties of an extension.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em provider} & The name of the extension provider, e.\+g. agora.\+io. \\
\hline
{\em extension} & The name of the extension, e.\+g. agora.\+beauty. \\
\hline
{\em extension\+Info} & The information for extension. \\
\hline

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!enableLoopbackRecording@{enableLoopbackRecording}}
\index{enableLoopbackRecording@{enableLoopbackRecording}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableLoopbackRecording()}{enableLoopbackRecording()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::enable\+Loopback\+Recording (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enabled,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{device\+Name = {\ttfamily NULL} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Enables loopback recording.

If you enable loopback recording, the output of the default sound card is mixed into the audio stream sent to the other end.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This method is for Windows only.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & Sets whether to enable/disable loopback recording.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Enable loopback recording.
\item false\+: (Default) Disable loopback recording. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em device\+Name} & Pointer to the device name of the sound card. The default value is N\+U\+LL (the default sound card).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This method is for mac\+OS and Windows only.
\item mac\+OS does not support loopback capturing of the default sound card. If you need to use this method, please use a virtual sound card and pass its name to the device\+Name parameter. Agora has tested and recommends using soundflower. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a95cdc3a285845cb35d56f470a0b488fb}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a95cdc3a285845cb35d56f470a0b488fb}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::register\+Extension (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{provider,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{extension,  }\item[{agora\+::media\+::\+M\+E\+D\+I\+A\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}]{type = {\ttfamily agora\+:\+:media\+:\+:UNKNOWN\+\_\+MEDIA\+\_\+SOURCE} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Registers an extension. Normally you should call this function immediately after engine initialization. Once an extension is registered, the S\+DK will automatically create and add it to the pipeline.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em provider} & The name of the extension provider, e.\+g. agora.\+io. \\
\hline
{\em extension} & The name of the extension, e.\+g. agora.\+beauty. \\
\hline
{\em type} & The source type of the extension, e.\+g. P\+R\+I\+M\+A\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+C\+A\+M\+E\+R\+A\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+CE. The default is U\+N\+K\+N\+O\+W\+N\+\_\+\+M\+E\+D\+I\+A\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+CE.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!enableExtension@{enableExtension}}
\index{enableExtension@{enableExtension}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableExtension()}{enableExtension()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::enable\+Extension (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{provider,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{extension,  }\item[{bool}]{enable = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{agora\+::media\+::\+M\+E\+D\+I\+A\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}]{type = {\ttfamily agora\+:\+:media\+:\+:UNKNOWN\+\_\+MEDIA\+\_\+SOURCE} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Enable/\+Disable an extension. By calling this function, you can dynamically enable/disable the extension without changing the pipeline. For example, enabling/disabling Extension\+\_\+A means the data will be adapted/bypassed by Extension\+\_\+A.

N\+O\+TE\+: For compatibility reasons, if you haven\textquotesingle{}t call register\+Extension, enable\+Extension will automatically register the specified extension. We suggest you call register\+Extension explicitly.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em provider} & The name of the extension provider, e.\+g. agora.\+io. \\
\hline
{\em extension} & The name of the extension, e.\+g. agora.\+beauty. \\
\hline
{\em enable} & Whether to enable the extension\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: (Default) Enable the extension.
\item false\+: Disable the extension. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em type} & The source type of the extension, e.\+g. P\+R\+I\+M\+A\+R\+Y\+\_\+\+C\+A\+M\+E\+R\+A\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+CE. The default is U\+N\+K\+N\+O\+W\+N\+\_\+\+M\+E\+D\+I\+A\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+CE.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!getCallId@{getCallId}}
\index{getCallId@{getCallId}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getCallId()}{getCallId()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::get\+Call\+Id (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1util_1_1_copyable_auto_ptr}{agora\+::util\+::\+A\+String}} \&}]{call\+Id }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Gets the current call ID.

When a user joins a channel on a client, a {\ttfamily call\+Id} is generated to identify the call.

After a call ends, you can call {\ttfamily rate} or {\ttfamily complain} to gather feedback from the customer. These methods require a {\ttfamily call\+Id} parameter. To use these feedback methods, call the this method first to retrieve the {\ttfamily call\+Id} during the call, and then pass the value as an argument in the {\ttfamily rate} or {\ttfamily complain} method after the call ends.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em call\+Id} & The reference to the call ID. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The call ID if the method call is successful.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a748c30a6339ec9798daa0d1b21585411}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a748c30a6339ec9798daa0d1b21585411}}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!startRtmpStreamWithoutTranscoding@{startRtmpStreamWithoutTranscoding}}
\index{startRtmpStreamWithoutTranscoding@{startRtmpStreamWithoutTranscoding}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startRtmpStreamWithoutTranscoding()}{startRtmpStreamWithoutTranscoding()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::start\+Rtmp\+Stream\+Without\+Transcoding (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{url }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Publishes the local stream without transcoding to a specified C\+DN live R\+T\+MP address. (C\+DN live only.)

The S\+DK returns the result of this method call in the on\+Stream\+Published callback.

The \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_acfc4de5d9454cad1dfd1d154e180d78c}{start\+Rtmp\+Stream\+Without\+Transcoding}} method call triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a01f3ce153df3a96703a0c9af934058f6}{on\+Rtmp\+Streaming\+State\+Changed}} callback on the local client to report the state of adding a local stream to the C\+DN. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Ensure that the user joins the channel before calling this method.
\item This method adds only one stream R\+T\+MP U\+RL address each time it is called.
\item The R\+T\+MP U\+RL address must not contain special characters, such as Chinese language characters.
\item This method applies to Live Broadcast only.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em url} & The C\+DN streaming U\+RL in the R\+T\+MP format. The maximum length of this parameter is 1024 bytes.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \#\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+NT (2)\+: The R\+T\+MP U\+RL address is N\+U\+LL or has a string length of 0.
\item \#\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+I\+A\+L\+I\+Z\+ED (7)\+: You have not initialized the R\+TC engine when publishing the stream.
\item \#\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+A\+L\+R\+E\+A\+D\+Y\+\_\+\+I\+N\+\_\+\+U\+SE (19)\+: This streaming U\+RL is already in use. Use a new streaming U\+RL for C\+DN streaming. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a0f91aa3af0a7c9a8428966028b5a010c}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a0f91aa3af0a7c9a8428966028b5a010c}}

Publishes the local stream with transcoding to a specified C\+DN live R\+T\+MP address. (C\+DN live only.)

The S\+DK returns the result of this method call in the on\+Stream\+Published callback.

\item Ensure that the user joins the channel before calling this method.
\item This method adds only one stream R\+T\+MP U\+RL address each time it is called.
\item The R\+T\+MP U\+RL address must not contain special characters, such as Chinese language characters.
\item This method applies to Live Broadcast only.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!stopRtmpStream@{stopRtmpStream}}
\index{stopRtmpStream@{stopRtmpStream}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{stopRtmpStream()}{stopRtmpStream()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::stop\+Rtmp\+Stream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{url }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Stop an R\+T\+MP stream with transcoding or without transcoding from the C\+DN. (C\+DN live only.)

This method removes the R\+T\+MP U\+RL address (added by the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_acfc4de5d9454cad1dfd1d154e180d78c}{start\+Rtmp\+Stream\+Without\+Transcoding}} method or \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a0f91aa3af0a7c9a8428966028b5a010c}{I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::start\+Rtmp\+Stream\+With\+Transcoding}} \char`\"{}start\+Rtmp\+Stream\+With\+Transcoding\char`\"{} method) from a C\+DN live stream. The S\+DK returns the result of this method call in the on\+Stream\+Unpublished callback.

The \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ab9807b2e5fb708d01066759af02cc630}{stop\+Rtmp\+Stream}} method call triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a01f3ce153df3a96703a0c9af934058f6}{on\+Rtmp\+Streaming\+State\+Changed}} callback on the local client to report the state of removing an R\+T\+MP stream from the C\+DN. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This method removes only one R\+T\+MP U\+RL address each time it is called.
\item The R\+T\+MP U\+RL address must not contain special characters, such as Chinese language characters.
\item This method applies to Live Broadcast only.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em url} & The R\+T\+MP U\+RL address to be removed. The maximum length of this parameter is 1024 bytes.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ad5ea5f0dfd8117f38d9c4b12fe01fece}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ad5ea5f0dfd8117f38d9c4b12fe01fece}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!enableEncryption@{enableEncryption}}
\index{enableEncryption@{enableEncryption}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableEncryption()}{enableEncryption()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::enable\+Encryption (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enabled,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_encryption_config}{Encryption\+Config}} \&}]{config }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Enables/\+Disables the built-\/in encryption.

In scenarios requiring high security, Agora recommends calling this method to enable the built-\/in encryption before joining a channel.

All users in the same channel must use the same encryption mode and encryption key. Once all users leave the channel, the encryption key of this channel is automatically cleared.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If you enable the built-\/in encryption, you cannot use the R\+T\+MP streaming function.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & Whether to enable the built-\/in encryption\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Enable the built-\/in encryption.
\item false\+: Disable the built-\/in encryption. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em config} & Configurations of built-\/in encryption schemas. See \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_encryption_config}{Encryption\+Config}}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item -\/2(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+NT)\+: An invalid parameter is used. Set the parameter with a valid value.
\item -\/4(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED)\+: The encryption mode is incorrect or the S\+DK fails to load the external encryption library. Check the enumeration or reload the external encryption library.
\item -\/7(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+I\+A\+L\+I\+Z\+ED)\+: The S\+DK is not initialized. Initialize the {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine}{I\+Rtc\+Engine}}} instance before calling this method. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a5a3f0168ca6e2e298e4677e9a8b9550a}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a5a3f0168ca6e2e298e4677e9a8b9550a}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!createDataStream@{createDataStream}}
\index{createDataStream@{createDataStream}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{createDataStream()}{createDataStream()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::create\+Data\+Stream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int $\ast$}]{stream\+Id,  }\item[{bool}]{reliable,  }\item[{bool}]{ordered }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Creates a data stream.

You can call this method to create a data stream and improve the reliability and ordering of data tranmission.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Ensure that you set the same value for {\ttfamily reliable} and {\ttfamily ordered}.
\item Each user can only create a maximum of 5 data streams during a Rtc\+Engine lifecycle.
\item The data channel allows a data delay of up to 5 seconds. If the receiver does not receive the data stream within 5 seconds, the data channel reports an error.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em stream\+Id} & The ID of the stream data. \\
\hline
 & {\em reliable} & Sets whether the recipients are guaranteed to receive the data stream from the sender within five seconds\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: The recipients receive the data stream from the sender within five seconds. If the recipient does not receive the data stream within five seconds, an error is reported to the application.
\item false\+: There is no guarantee that the recipients receive the data stream within five seconds and no error message is reported for any delay or missing data stream. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
 & {\em ordered} & Sets whether the recipients receive the data stream in the sent order\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: The recipients receive the data stream in the sent order.
\item false\+: The recipients do not receive the data stream in the sent order.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_acf920f7dc761e2d7b7e28006c74238b7}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_acf920f7dc761e2d7b7e28006c74238b7}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!createDataStream@{createDataStream}}
\index{createDataStream@{createDataStream}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7006214f7ca3c08d83cc0a4ebcb9febc}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7006214f7ca3c08d83cc0a4ebcb9febc}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!sendStreamMessage@{sendStreamMessage}}
\index{sendStreamMessage@{sendStreamMessage}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sendStreamMessage()}{sendStreamMessage()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::send\+Stream\+Message (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{stream\+Id,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{data,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{length }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sends a data stream.

After calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a5a3f0168ca6e2e298e4677e9a8b9550a}{create\+Data\+Stream}}, you can call this method to send a data stream to all users in the channel.

The S\+DK has the following restrictions on this method\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Up to 60 packets can be sent per second in a channel with each packet having a maximum size of 1 KB.
\item Each client can send up to 30 KB of data per second.
\item Each user can have up to five data streams simultaneously.
\end{DoxyItemize}

After the remote user receives the data stream within 5 seconds, the S\+DK triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a0add560882999732aec21098c29280e0}{on\+Stream\+Message}} callback on the remote client. After the remote user does not receive the data stream within 5 seconds, the S\+DK triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a3af56e33ca95ccc6b9dce4b2a51c2b33}{on\+Stream\+Message\+Error}} callback on the remote client.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Call this method after calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a5a3f0168ca6e2e298e4677e9a8b9550a}{create\+Data\+Stream}}.
\item This method applies only to the {\ttfamily C\+O\+M\+M\+U\+N\+I\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON} profile or to the hosts in the {\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} profile. If an audience in the {\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} profile calls this method, the audience may be switched to a host.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em stream\+Id} & The ID of the stream data. \\
\hline
{\em data} & The data stream. \\
\hline
{\em length} & The length (byte) of the data stream.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a4caf3477d91c3aa0ea8b178948cad8d5}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a4caf3477d91c3aa0ea8b178948cad8d5}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!addVideoWatermark@{addVideoWatermark}}
\index{addVideoWatermark@{addVideoWatermark}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addVideoWatermark()}{addVideoWatermark()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::add\+Video\+Watermark (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_rtc_image}{Rtc\+Image}} \&}]{watermark }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

{\bfseries{D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED}} Adds a watermark image to the local video or C\+DN live stream.

This method is not recommend, Use \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a36e51346ec3bd5a7370d7c70d58d9394}{add\+Video\+Watermark}}2 instead.

This method adds a P\+NG watermark image to the local video stream for the recording device, channel audience, and C\+DN live audience to view and capture.

To add the P\+NG file to the C\+DN live publishing stream, see the set\+Live\+Transcoding method.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em watermark} & Pointer to the watermark image to be added to the local video stream. See \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_rtc_image}{Rtc\+Image}}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The U\+RL descriptions are different for the local video and C\+DN live streams\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item In a local video stream, {\ttfamily url} in \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_rtc_image}{Rtc\+Image}} refers to the absolute path of the added watermark image file in the local video stream.
\item In a C\+DN live stream, {\ttfamily url} in \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_rtc_image}{Rtc\+Image}} refers to the U\+RL address of the added watermark image in the C\+DN live broadcast.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item The source file of the watermark image must be in the P\+NG file format. If the width and height of the P\+NG file differ from your settings in this method, the P\+NG file will be cropped to conform to your settings.
\item The Agora S\+DK supports adding only one watermark image onto a local video or C\+DN live stream. The newly added watermark image replaces the previous one.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a36e51346ec3bd5a7370d7c70d58d9394}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a36e51346ec3bd5a7370d7c70d58d9394}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!addVideoWatermark@{addVideoWatermark}}
\index{addVideoWatermark@{addVideoWatermark}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addVideoWatermark()}{addVideoWatermark()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::add\+Video\+Watermark (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{watermark\+Url,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_watermark_options}{Watermark\+Options}} \&}]{options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Adds a watermark image to the local video.

This method adds a P\+NG watermark image to the local video in a live broadcast. Once the watermark image is added, all the audience in the channel (C\+DN audience included), and the recording device can see and capture it. Agora supports adding only one watermark image onto the local video, and the newly watermark image replaces the previous one.

The watermark position depends on the settings in the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a9bcbdcee0b5c52f96b32baec1922cf2e}{set\+Video\+Encoder\+Configuration}} method\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If the orientation mode of the encoding video is \#\+O\+R\+I\+E\+N\+T\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+F\+I\+X\+E\+D\+\_\+\+L\+A\+N\+D\+S\+C\+A\+PE, or the landscape mode in \#\+O\+R\+I\+E\+N\+T\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+A\+D\+A\+P\+T\+I\+VE, the watermark uses the landscape orientation.
\item If the orientation mode of the encoding video is \#\+O\+R\+I\+E\+N\+T\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+F\+I\+X\+E\+D\+\_\+\+P\+O\+R\+T\+R\+A\+IT, or the portrait mode in \#\+O\+R\+I\+E\+N\+T\+A\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+A\+D\+A\+P\+T\+I\+VE, the watermark uses the portrait orientation.
\item When setting the watermark position, the region must be less than the dimensions set in the {\ttfamily set\+Video\+Encoder\+Configuration} method. Otherwise, the watermark image will be cropped.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Ensure that you have called the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7d35fc62d74685d25636f04b04051958}{enable\+Video}} method to enable the video module before calling this method.
\item If you only want to add a watermark image to the local video for the audience in the C\+DN live broadcast channel to see and capture, you can call this method or the set\+Live\+Transcoding method.
\item This method supports adding a watermark image in the P\+NG file format only. Supported pixel formats of the P\+NG image are R\+G\+BA, R\+GB, Palette, Gray, and Alpha\+\_\+gray.
\item If the dimensions of the P\+NG image differ from your settings in this method, the image will be cropped or zoomed to conform to your settings.
\item If you have enabled the local video preview by calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_aabd5f0d670a6cd26badc316083519512}{start\+Preview}} method, you can use the {\ttfamily visible\+In\+Preview} member in the \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_watermark_options}{Watermark\+Options}} class to set whether or not the watermark is visible in preview.
\item If you have enabled the mirror mode for the local video, the watermark on the local video is also mirrored. To avoid mirroring the watermark, Agora recommends that you do not use the mirror and watermark functions for the local video at the same time. You can implement the watermark function in your application layer.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em watermark\+Url} & The local file path of the watermark image to be added. This method supports adding a watermark image from the local absolute or relative file path. \\
\hline
{\em options} & Pointer to the watermark\textquotesingle{}s options to be added. See \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_watermark_options}{Watermark\+Options}} for more infomation.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
int
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_aea42a1ea8b83bc807f68526945f40ec6}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_aea42a1ea8b83bc807f68526945f40ec6}}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!enableWebSdkInteroperability@{enableWebSdkInteroperability}}
\index{enableWebSdkInteroperability@{enableWebSdkInteroperability}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableWebSdkInteroperability()}{enableWebSdkInteroperability()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::enable\+Web\+Sdk\+Interoperability (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Enables interoperability with the Agora Web S\+DK (Live Broadcast only).

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000029}{Deprecated}}]The Agora NG S\+DK enables the interoperablity with the Web S\+DK.\end{DoxyRefDesc}


Use this method when the channel profile is Live Broadcast. Interoperability with the Agora Web S\+DK is enabled by default when the channel profile is Communication.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: (Default) Enable interoperability with the Agora Native S\+DK.
\item false\+: Disable interoperability with the Agora Native S\+DK.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure.

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!sendCustomReportMessage@{sendCustomReportMessage}}
\index{sendCustomReportMessage@{sendCustomReportMessage}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sendCustomReportMessage()}{sendCustomReportMessage()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::send\+Custom\+Report\+Message (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{id,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{category,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{event,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{label,  }\item[{int}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Agora supports reporting and analyzing customized messages.

This function is in the beta stage with a free trial. The ability provided in its beta test version is reporting a maximum of 10 message pieces within 6 seconds, with each message piece not exceeding 256 bytes.

To try out this function, contact \href{mailto:support@agora.io}{\texttt{ support@agora.\+io}} and discuss the format of customized messages with us. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a84dbf06de1d769b63200d7ec0289cca0}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a84dbf06de1d769b63200d7ec0289cca0}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!registerMediaMetadataObserver@{registerMediaMetadataObserver}}
\index{registerMediaMetadataObserver@{registerMediaMetadataObserver}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{registerMediaMetadataObserver()}{registerMediaMetadataObserver()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::register\+Media\+Metadata\+Observer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_metadata_observer}{I\+Metadata\+Observer}} $\ast$}]{observer,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_metadata_observer_a50ad8779d161456fc709d947b8c7c544}{I\+Metadata\+Observer\+::\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}}}]{type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Registers the metadata observer.

You need to implement the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_metadata_observer}{I\+Metadata\+Observer}} class and specify the metadata type in this method. This method enables you to add synchronized metadata in the video stream for more diversified live interactive streaming, such as sending shopping links, digital coupons, and online quizzes.

A successful call of this method triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_metadata_observer_aa1d7b729f373d985a5bbdd855c4e85d5}{get\+Max\+Metadata\+Size}} callback.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Call this method before the {\ttfamily join\+Channel} method.
\item This method applies to the {\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} channel profile.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em observer} & \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_metadata_observer}{I\+Metadata\+Observer}}. \\
\hline
{\em type} & The metadata type. See \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_metadata_observer_a50ad8779d161456fc709d947b8c7c544}{M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+T\+A\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}}. The S\+DK supports V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+A\+D\+A\+TA (0) only for now.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::start\+Audio\+Frame\+Dump (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{channel\+\_\+id,  }\item[{uid\+\_\+t}]{uid,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{location,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{uuid,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{passwd,  }\item[{long}]{duration\+\_\+ms,  }\item[{bool}]{auto\+\_\+upload }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1_optional}{Optional}} {\ttfamily location} is\+: \char`\"{}pre\+\_\+apm\+\_\+proc\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}apm\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}pre\+\_\+send\+\_\+proc\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}filter\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}enc\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}tx\+\_\+mixer\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}at\+\_\+record\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}atw\+\_\+record\char`\"{} for audio sending. \char`\"{}dec\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}mixed\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}play\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}rx\+\_\+mixer\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}playback\+\_\+mixer\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}pcm\+\_\+source\+\_\+playback\+\_\+mixer\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}pre\+\_\+play\+\_\+proc\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}at\+\_\+playout\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}atw\+\_\+playout\char`\"{} for audio receiving. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a273c143c4df3e74b9aea29d4027b2e9c}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a273c143c4df3e74b9aea29d4027b2e9c}}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setAINSMode@{setAINSMode}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+A\+I\+N\+S\+Mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enabled,  }\item[{A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+A\+I\+N\+S\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}]{mode }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

\item false\+: Disables the A\+I\+NS. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em mode} & The preset A\+I\+NS mode, range is \mbox{[}0,1,2\mbox{]}\+: 0\+: A\+I\+NS mode with soft suppression level. 1\+: A\+I\+NS mode with aggressive suppression level. 2\+: A\+I\+NS mode with aggressive suppression level and low algorithm latency.\\
