\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a0d44b74ced4005ee86353c13186f870d}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a0d44b74ced4005ee86353c13186f870d}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!registerLocalUserAccount@{registerLocalUserAccount}}
\index{registerLocalUserAccount@{registerLocalUserAccount}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{registerLocalUserAccount()}{registerLocalUserAccount()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::register\+Local\+User\+Account (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{app\+Id,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{user\+Account }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Registers a user account.

Once registered, the user account can be used to identify the local user when the user joins the channel. After the user successfully registers a user account, the S\+DK triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a919404869f86412e1945c730e5219b20}{on\+Local\+User\+Registered}} callback on the local client, reporting the user ID and user account of the local user.

To join a channel with a user account, you can choose either of the following\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Call the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a0d44b74ced4005ee86353c13186f870d}{register\+Local\+User\+Account}} method to create a user account, and then the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a14f8c308c6c57c55653552b939a8527a}{join\+Channel\+With\+User\+Account}} method to join the channel.
\item Call the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a14f8c308c6c57c55653552b939a8527a}{join\+Channel\+With\+User\+Account}} method to join the channel.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The difference between the two is that for the former, the time elapsed between calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a14f8c308c6c57c55653552b939a8527a}{join\+Channel\+With\+User\+Account}} method and joining the channel is shorter than the latter.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Ensure that you set the {\ttfamily user\+Account} parameter. Otherwise, this method does not take effect.
\item Ensure that the value of the {\ttfamily user\+Account} parameter is unique in the channel.
\item To ensure smooth communication, use the same parameter type to identify the user. For example, if a user joins the channel with a user ID, then ensure all the other users use the user ID too. The same applies to the user account. If a user joins the channel with the Agora Web S\+DK, ensure that the uid of the user is set to the same parameter type.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em app\+Id} & The App ID of your project. \\
\hline
{\em user\+Account} & The user account. The maximum length of this parameter is 255 bytes. Ensure that you set this parameter and do not set it as null. Supported character scopes are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item All lowercase English letters\+: a to z.
\item All uppercase English letters\+: A to Z.
\item All numeric characters\+: 0 to 9.
\item The space character.
\item Punctuation characters and other symbols, including\+: \char`\"{}!\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\#\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\%\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\&\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}(\char`\"{}, \char`\"{})\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}-\/\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+:\char`\"{}, \char`\"{};\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$<$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}=\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}.\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$>$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}?\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}@\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{[}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{]}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$^\wedge$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+\_\+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{} \{\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\vert$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\sim$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{},\char`\"{}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a14f8c308c6c57c55653552b939a8527a}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a14f8c308c6c57c55653552b939a8527a}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!joinChannelWithUserAccount@{joinChannelWithUserAccount}}
\index{joinChannelWithUserAccount@{joinChannelWithUserAccount}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{joinChannelWithUserAccount()}{joinChannelWithUserAccount()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::join\+Channel\+With\+User\+Account (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{token,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{channel\+Id,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{user\+Account }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Joins the channel with a user account.

After the user successfully joins the channel, the S\+DK triggers the following callbacks\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The local client\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a919404869f86412e1945c730e5219b20}{on\+Local\+User\+Registered}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_aafceb1f91ae9bd82317bf25981e6851b}{on\+Join\+Channel\+Success}} .
\item The remote client\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a985a675469baf9d54feb8781732e0ca8}{on\+User\+Joined}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_ad086cc4d8e5555cc75a0ab264c16d5ff}{on\+User\+Info\+Updated}} , if the user joining the channel is in the {\ttfamily C\+O\+M\+M\+U\+N\+I\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON} profile, or is a host in the {\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} profile.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
To ensure smooth communication, use the same parameter type to identify the user. For example, if a user joins the channel with a user ID, then ensure all the other users use the user ID too. The same applies to the user account. If a user joins the channel with the Agora Web S\+DK, ensure that the uid of the user is set to the same parameter type.
\end{DoxyNote}

\item For high-\/security requirements\+: Set it as the token generated at your server. For details, see \href{https://docs.agora.io/en/Voice/token?platform=All\%20Platforms\#get-a-token}{\texttt{ Get a token}}.

Joins the channel with a user account.

After the user successfully joins the channel, the S\+DK triggers the following callbacks\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The local client\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a919404869f86412e1945c730e5219b20}{on\+Local\+User\+Registered}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_aafceb1f91ae9bd82317bf25981e6851b}{on\+Join\+Channel\+Success}} .
\item The remote client\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a985a675469baf9d54feb8781732e0ca8}{on\+User\+Joined}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_ad086cc4d8e5555cc75a0ab264c16d5ff}{on\+User\+Info\+Updated}} , if the user joining the channel is in the {\ttfamily C\+O\+M\+M\+U\+N\+I\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON} profile, or is a host in the {\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} profile.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
To ensure smooth communication, use the same parameter type to identify the user. For example, if a user joins the channel with a user ID, then ensure all the other users use the user ID too. The same applies to the user account. If a user joins the channel with the Agora Web S\+DK, ensure that the uid of the user is set to the same parameter type.
\end{DoxyNote}

\item For high-\/security requirements\+: Set it as the token generated at your server. For details, see \href{https://docs.agora.io/en/Voice/token?platform=All\%20Platforms\#get-a-token}{\texttt{ Get a token}}.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item All lowercase English letters\+: a to z.
\item All uppercase English letters\+: A to Z.
\item All numeric characters\+: 0 to 9.
\item The space character.
\item Punctuation characters and other symbols, including\+: \char`\"{}!\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\#\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\%\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\&\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}(\char`\"{}, \char`\"{})\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}-\/\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+:\char`\"{}, \char`\"{};\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$<$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}=\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}.\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$>$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}?\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}@\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{[}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{]}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$^\wedge$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+\_\+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{} \{\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\vert$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\sim$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{},\char`\"{}. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em user\+Account} & The user account. The maximum length of this parameter is 255 bytes. Ensure that you set this parameter and do not set it as null. Supported character scopes are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item All lowercase English letters\+: a to z.
\item All uppercase English letters\+: A to Z.
\item All numeric characters\+: 0 to 9.
\item The space character.
\item Punctuation characters and other symbols, including\+: \char`\"{}!\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\#\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\%\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\&\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}(\char`\"{}, \char`\"{})\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}-\/\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+:\char`\"{}, \char`\"{};\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$<$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}=\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}.\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$>$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}?\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}@\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{[}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{]}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$^\wedge$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+\_\+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{} \{\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\vert$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\sim$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{},\char`\"{}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a124148443b2438da668fb683e96a9f41}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a124148443b2438da668fb683e96a9f41}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!joinChannelWithUserAccountEx@{joinChannelWithUserAccountEx}}
\index{joinChannelWithUserAccountEx@{joinChannelWithUserAccountEx}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{joinChannelWithUserAccountEx()}{joinChannelWithUserAccountEx()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::join\+Channel\+With\+User\+Account\+Ex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{token,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{channel\+Id,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{user\+Account,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_channel_media_options}{Channel\+Media\+Options}} \&}]{options,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler}{I\+Rtc\+Engine\+Event\+Handler}} $\ast$}]{event\+Handler }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Joins the channel with a user account.

After the user successfully joins the channel, the S\+DK triggers the following callbacks\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The local client\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a919404869f86412e1945c730e5219b20}{on\+Local\+User\+Registered}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_aafceb1f91ae9bd82317bf25981e6851b}{on\+Join\+Channel\+Success}} .
\item The remote client\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a985a675469baf9d54feb8781732e0ca8}{on\+User\+Joined}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_ad086cc4d8e5555cc75a0ab264c16d5ff}{on\+User\+Info\+Updated}} , if the user joining the channel is in the {\ttfamily C\+O\+M\+M\+U\+N\+I\+C\+A\+T\+I\+ON} profile, or is a host in the {\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} profile.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
To ensure smooth communication, use the same parameter type to identify the user. For example, if a user joins the channel with a user ID, then ensure all the other users use the user ID too. The same applies to the user account. If a user joins the channel with the Agora Web S\+DK, ensure that the uid of the user is set to the same parameter type.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em token} & The token generated at your server\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item For low-\/security requirements\+: You can use the temporary token generated at Console. For details, see \href{https://docs.agora.io/en/Voice/token?platform=All\%20Platforms\#get-a-temporary-token}{\texttt{ Get a temporary toke}}.
\item For high-\/security requirements\+: Set it as the token generated at your server. For details, see \href{https://docs.agora.io/en/Voice/token?platform=All\%20Platforms\#get-a-token}{\texttt{ Get a token}}. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item All lowercase English letters\+: a to z.
\item All uppercase English letters\+: A to Z.
\item All numeric characters\+: 0 to 9.
\item The space character.
\item Punctuation characters and other symbols, including\+: \char`\"{}!\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\#\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\%\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\&\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}(\char`\"{}, \char`\"{})\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}-\/\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+:\char`\"{}, \char`\"{};\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$<$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}=\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}.\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$>$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}?\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}@\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{[}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{]}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$^\wedge$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+\_\+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{} \{\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\vert$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\sim$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{},\char`\"{}.

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!getUserInfoByUserAccount@{getUserInfoByUserAccount}}
\index{getUserInfoByUserAccount@{getUserInfoByUserAccount}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getUserInfoByUserAccount()}{getUserInfoByUserAccount()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::get\+User\+Info\+By\+User\+Account (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{user\+Account,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_user_info}{rtc\+::\+User\+Info}} $\ast$}]{user\+Info }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Gets the user information by passing in the user account.

After a remote user joins the channel, the S\+DK gets the user ID and user account of the remote user, caches them in a mapping table object ({\ttfamily user\+Info}), and triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_ad086cc4d8e5555cc75a0ab264c16d5ff}{on\+User\+Info\+Updated}} callback on the local client.

After receiving the o\mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_ad086cc4d8e5555cc75a0ab264c16d5ff}{on\+User\+Info\+Updated}} callback, you can call this method to get the user ID of the remote user from the {\ttfamily user\+Info} object by passing in the user account.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em user\+Account} & The user account of the user. Ensure that you set this parameter. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em user\+Info} & A user\+Info object that identifies the user\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Input\+: A user\+Info object.
\item Output\+: A user\+Info object that contains the user account and user ID of the user.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

After receiving the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_ad086cc4d8e5555cc75a0ab264c16d5ff}{on\+User\+Info\+Updated}} callback, you can call this method to get the user account of the remote user from the {\ttfamily user\+Info} object by passing in the user ID.

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!startOrUpdateChannelMediaRelay@{startOrUpdateChannelMediaRelay}}
\index{startOrUpdateChannelMediaRelay@{startOrUpdateChannelMediaRelay}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startOrUpdateChannelMediaRelay()}{startOrUpdateChannelMediaRelay()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::start\+Or\+Update\+Channel\+Media\+Relay (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_channel_media_relay_configuration}{Channel\+Media\+Relay\+Configuration}} \&}]{configuration }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Starts relaying media streams across channels or updates the channels for media relay.

After a successful method call, the S\+DK triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a1891ed124db5f74747e74ca3b3eb23e9}{on\+Channel\+Media\+Relay\+State\+Changed}} callback, and this callback return the state of the media stream relay.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a1891ed124db5f74747e74ca3b3eb23e9}{on\+Channel\+Media\+Relay\+State\+Changed}} callback returns \#\+R\+E\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+U\+N\+N\+I\+NG (2) and \#\+R\+E\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+OK (0), the host starts sending data to the destination channel.
\item If the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a1891ed124db5f74747e74ca3b3eb23e9}{on\+Channel\+Media\+Relay\+State\+Changed}} callback returns \#\+R\+E\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+I\+L\+U\+RE (3), an exception occurs during the media stream relay.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Call this method after the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_adc937172e59bd2695ea171553a88188c}{join\+Channel}} method.
\item This method takes effect only when you are a host in a {\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} channel.
\item Contact \href{mailto:sales-us@agora.io}{\texttt{ sales-\/us@agora.\+io}} before implementing this function.
\item We do not support string user accounts in this A\+PI.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v4.\+2.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em configuration} & The configuration of the media stream relay\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_channel_media_relay_configuration}{Channel\+Media\+Relay\+Configuration}}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\item $<$ 0\+: Failure.
\begin{DoxyItemize}

\item -\/2(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+NT)\+: The argument is invalid.
\item -\/5(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+R\+E\+F\+U\+S\+ED)\+: The request is rejected.
\item -\/8(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+TE)\+: The current status is invalid, only allowed to be called when the role is the broadcaster. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ab4a1c52a83a08f7dacab6de36f4681b8}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ab4a1c52a83a08f7dacab6de36f4681b8}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!stopChannelMediaRelay@{stopChannelMediaRelay}}
\index{stopChannelMediaRelay@{stopChannelMediaRelay}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{stopChannelMediaRelay()}{stopChannelMediaRelay()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::stop\+Channel\+Media\+Relay (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Stops the media stream relay.

Once the relay stops, the host quits all the destination channels.

After a successful method call, the S\+DK triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a1891ed124db5f74747e74ca3b3eb23e9}{on\+Channel\+Media\+Relay\+State\+Changed}} callback. If the callback returns \#\+R\+E\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+I\+D\+LE (0) and \#\+R\+E\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+OK (0), the host successfully stops the relay.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If the method call fails, the S\+DK triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a1891ed124db5f74747e74ca3b3eb23e9}{on\+Channel\+Media\+Relay\+State\+Changed}} callback with the \#\+R\+E\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+S\+E\+R\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+P\+O\+N\+SE (2) or \#\+R\+E\+L\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+S\+E\+R\+V\+E\+R\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+L\+O\+ST (8) state code. You can leave the channel by calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a51c12d209373650638bfd82e28777081}{leave\+Channel}} method, and the media stream relay automatically stops.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item -\/1(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+F\+A\+I\+L\+ED)\+: A general error occurs (no specified reason).
\item -\/2(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+NT)\+: The argument is invalid.
\item -\/5(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+R\+E\+F\+U\+S\+ED)\+: The request is rejected.
\item -\/7(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+I\+A\+L\+I\+Z\+ED)\+: cross channel media streams are not relayed. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a6761e2f090290567d1f592841c40d96c}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a6761e2f090290567d1f592841c40d96c}}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setDirectCdnStreamingAudioConfiguration@{setDirectCdnStreamingAudioConfiguration}}
\index{setDirectCdnStreamingAudioConfiguration@{setDirectCdnStreamingAudioConfiguration}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setDirectCdnStreamingAudioConfiguration()}{setDirectCdnStreamingAudioConfiguration()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Direct\+Cdn\+Streaming\+Audio\+Configuration (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}]{profile }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!takeSnapshot@{takeSnapshot}}
\index{takeSnapshot@{takeSnapshot}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{takeSnapshot()}{takeSnapshot()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::take\+Snapshot (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uid\+\_\+t}]{uid,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{file\+Path }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Takes a snapshot of a video stream.

This method takes a snapshot of a video stream from the specified user, generates a J\+PG image, and saves it to the specified path.

The method is asynchronous, and the S\+DK has not taken the snapshot when the method call returns. After a successful method call, the S\+DK triggers the {\ttfamily on\+Snapshot\+Taken} callback to report whether the snapshot is successfully taken, as well as the details for that snapshot.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Call this method after joining a channel.
\item This method takes a snapshot of the published video stream specified in {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_channel_media_options}{Channel\+Media\+Options}}}.
\item If the user\textquotesingle{}s video has been preprocessed, for example, watermarked or beautified, the resulting snapshot includes the pre-\/processing effect.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em uid} & The user ID. Set uid as 0 if you want to take a snapshot of the local user\textquotesingle{}s video. \\
\hline
{\em file\+Path} & The local path (including filename extensions) of the snapshot. For example\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Windows\+: {\ttfamily C\+:\textbackslash{}Users\textbackslash{}$<$user\+\_\+name$>$\textbackslash{}App\+Data\textbackslash{}Local\textbackslash{}Agora\textbackslash{}$<$process\+\_\+name$>$\textbackslash{}example.\+jpg}
\item i\+OS\+: {\ttfamily /\+App Sandbox/\+Library/\+Caches/example.\+jpg}
\item mac\+OS\+: {\ttfamily ～/\+Library/\+Logs/example.jpg}
\item Android\+: {\ttfamily /storage/emulated/0/\+Android/data/$<$package name$>$/files/example.jpg}
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Ensure that the path you specify exists and is writable. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0 \+: Success.
\item $<$ 0 \+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac0caaeeaaffaebc35cd2312d05f85b93}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac0caaeeaaffaebc35cd2312d05f85b93}}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setCloudProxy@{setCloudProxy}}
\index{setCloudProxy@{setCloudProxy}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setCloudProxy()}{setCloudProxy()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Cloud\+Proxy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{C\+L\+O\+U\+D\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+X\+Y\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}]{proxy\+Type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets the Agora cloud proxy service.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v3.\+3.\+0
\end{DoxySince}
When the user\textquotesingle{}s firewall restricts the IP address and port, refer to {\itshape Use Cloud Proxy} to add the specific IP addresses and ports to the firewall allowlist; then, call this method to enable the cloud proxy and set the {\ttfamily proxy\+Type} parameter as {\ttfamily U\+D\+P\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+X\+Y(1)}, which is the cloud proxy for the U\+DP protocol.

After a successfully cloud proxy connection, the S\+DK triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_af409b2e721d345a65a2c600cea2f5eb4}{on\+Connection\+State\+Changed}} (C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+NG, C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+C\+H\+A\+N\+G\+E\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+T\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+X\+Y\+\_\+\+S\+E\+R\+V\+ER) callback.

To disable the cloud proxy that has been set, call {\ttfamily set\+Cloud\+Proxy(\+N\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+X\+Y)}. To change the cloud proxy type that has been set, call {\ttfamily set\+Cloud\+Proxy(\+N\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+X\+Y)} first, and then call {\ttfamily set\+Cloud\+Proxy}, and pass the value that you expect in {\ttfamily proxy\+Type}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Agora recommends that you call this method before joining the channel or after leaving the channel.
\item For the S\+DK v3.\+3.\+x, the services for pushing streams to C\+DN and co-\/hosting across channels are not available when you use the cloud proxy for the U\+DP protocol. For the S\+DK v3.\+4.\+0 and later, the services for pushing streams to C\+DN and co-\/hosting across channels are not available when the user is in a network environment with a firewall and uses the cloud proxy for the U\+DP protocol.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em proxy\+Type} & The cloud proxy type, see \#\+C\+L\+O\+U\+D\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+X\+Y\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE. This parameter is required, and the S\+DK reports an error if you do not pass in a value.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily -\/2(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+NT)}\+: The parameter is invalid.
\item {\ttfamily -\/7(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+I\+A\+L\+I\+Z\+ED)}\+: The S\+DK is not initialized. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a00358b706ea747938165984198b16009}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a00358b706ea747938165984198b16009}}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!enableWirelessAccelerate@{enableWirelessAccelerate}}
\index{enableWirelessAccelerate@{enableWirelessAccelerate}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableWirelessAccelerate()}{enableWirelessAccelerate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::enable\+Wireless\+Accelerate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Turns W\+I\+FI acceleration on or off.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This method is called before and after joining a channel.
\item Users check the W\+I\+FI router app for information about acceleration. Therefore, if this interface is invoked, the caller accepts that the caller\textquotesingle{}s name will be displayed to the user in the W\+I\+FI router application on behalf of the caller.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true：\+Turn W\+I\+FI acceleration on.
\item false：\+Turn W\+I\+FI acceleration off.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!startMediaRenderingTracing@{startMediaRenderingTracing}}
\index{startMediaRenderingTracing@{startMediaRenderingTracing}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startMediaRenderingTracing()}{startMediaRenderingTracing()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::start\+Media\+Rendering\+Tracing (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}



Start tracing media rendering events. 

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v4.\+1.\+1 @discussion
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item S\+DK will trace media rendering events when this A\+PI is called.
\item The tracing result can be obtained through callback {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_af157b707afd93a5b0ab39569e46a6cd4}{I\+Rtc\+Engine\+Event\+Handler\+::on\+Video\+Rendering\+Tracing\+Result}}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxySince}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item By default, S\+DK will trace media rendering events when {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_adc937172e59bd2695ea171553a88188c}{I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::join\+Channel}}} is called.
\item The start point of event tracing will be reset after leaving channel. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item -\/7(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+I\+A\+L\+I\+Z\+ED)\+: The S\+DK is not initialized. Initialize the {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine}{I\+Rtc\+Engine}}} instance before calling this method. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

Enable instant media rendering. 

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v4.\+1.\+1 @discussion

\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Once enable this mode, we should destroy rtc engine to disable it.
\item Enable this mode, will sacrifice some part of experience.

\end{DoxyItemize}
